// Commands
             say : Sends a message to a player as the server
  setfetterlevel : Sets your fetter level for your current active character
   setworldlevel : Sets your world level (Relog to see proper effects)
        setstats : Sets fight property for your current active character
            give : Gives an item to you or the specified player
        language : Display or change current language
         giveall : Gives all items
           quest : Add or finish quests
     unlocktower : Unlock all levels of tower
         killall : Kill all entities
     changescene : Changes your scene
        setstats : Sets fight property for your current active character
          talent : Set talent level for your current active character
         weather : Changes the weather
     unlocktower : Unlock all levels of tower
            give : Gives an item to you or the specified player
            give : Gives an item to you or the specified player
            list : List online players
   killcharacter : Kills the players current character
     changescene : Changes your scene
            list : List online players
         giveall : Gives all items
         giveart : Gives the player a specified artifact
        givechar : Gives the player a specified character
           tpall : Teleports all players in your world to your position
            stop : Stops the server
        position : Get coordinates
      resetconst : Resets the constellation level on your current active character, you will need to relog after using the command to see any changes
      resetconst : Resets the constellation level on your current active character, you will need to relog after using the command to see any changes
       broadcast : Sends a message to all the players
            drop : Drops an item near you
            drop : Drops an item near you
             say : Sends a message to a player as the server
        givechar : Gives the player a specified character
        teleport : Change the player's position
         giveart : Gives the player a specified artifact
  setfetterlevel : Sets your fetter level for your current active character
   setworldlevel : Sets your world level (Relog to see proper effects)
          reload : Reload server config
        position : Get coordinates
            heal : Heal all characters in your current team.
   killcharacter : Kills the players current character
        sendmail : Sends mail to the specified user. The usage of this command changes based on its composition state
        language : Display or change current language
    enterdungeon : Enter a dungeon
         godmode : Prevents you from taking damage. Defaults to toggle.
       broadcast : Sends a message to all the players
            coop : Forces someone to join the world of others
            drop : Drops an item near you
         restart : Restarts the current session
            give : Gives an item to you or the specified player
  setfetterlevel : Sets your fetter level for your current active character
            heal : Heal all characters in your current team.
           clear : Deletes unequipped unlocked items, including yellow rarity ones from your inventory
             say : Sends a message to a player as the server
      permission : Grants or removes a permission for a user
       resetshop : Reset target player's shop refresh time
            team : Modify your team manually.
   killcharacter : Kills the players current character
    enterdungeon : Enter a dungeon
            help : Sends the help message or shows information about a specified command
           spawn : Spawns an entity near you
            kick : Kicks the specified player from the server (WIP)
             say : Sends a message to a player as the server
         weather : Changes the weather
        teleport : Change the player's position
       nostamina : Keep your endurance to the maximum.
         account : Modify user accounts
